88th Standing Committee Meeting of the Central Executive Committee

The Central Executive Committee held its 88th Standing Committee Meeting at 3 PM on the 21st. Attendees included Hu Hanmin, Tan Yankai, Dai Chuanxian (Chen Guofu was excused due to business). Those present by invitation included Miao Bin, Shao Yuanchong, Jiao Yitang, Li Wenfan, Ke Xinge, Zhou Qigang, Chen Yaoyuan, Zhang Daofan, Wu Jingheng, Liu Luyin, Lin Sen, Gu Yingfen, Enhe Batu, and Chen Lifu. Hu Hanmin chaired the meeting. The resolutions are as follows: (1) It was resolved to designate Qian Dajun, Zhao Jinsha, Zhang Liangxin, Mao Hongfan, and Qin as members of the Special Party Department Supervisory Committee of the Wuhan Branch of the Central Military Academy, with Li Ximao and Li Mo as alternate supervisory committee members. (2) A proposal by Chiang Kai-shek and others to change the name of the phonetic alphabet to phonetic symbols and to formulate implementation measures was approved. (3) It was resolved to add Chen Zhaoqi and Xia Tianyan as compilers to the Party History Compilation Committee. (4) Eleven cases of disciplinary action against party members sent by the Central Supervisory Committee were reviewed. Those permanently expelled from the party were Zhang Zizheng (Gaotang, Shandong), Liu Shaoi (Shanxi), and Ren Bingxin (Yixing, Jiangsu). Those expelled from the party were Cheng Zhihong (Juxian, Shandong), Tang Peifang (Shanghai), Jiao Zongkong (Anguo, Hebei), Gu Zhibin (Qingpu, Jiangsu), and Zhu Yucai and Fan Fayi (Jiangsu). Those expelled from the party for one year was Lei Shi (Shanghai). All were resolved to be handled accordingly.

Commemorative Week of the Central Government and National Government

▲Central Party Headquarters: At 9 AM on the 21st, the Central Party Headquarters held the 56th Sun Yat-sen Memorial Week in the auditorium. Approximately five or six hundred people attended, including central committee members, officials from various departments and commissions, and guests. Dai Chuanxian chaired the meeting. After the ceremony, the chairman reported, stating briefly that there were several particularly important events recently: (1) The Central Government convened a National Training Conference. (2) The Capital Construction Committee held its first plenary meeting. (3) The Second National Education Conference was convened. (4) The National Games were held in Hangzhou. (5) The National Boy Scout General Review was held. The above matters are all related to the fundamental plans of the party and the nation. I will now highlight their essentials as a contribution, hoping that all comrades will pay attention. (1) The responsibility for training work is extremely important, but in fact, there are various difficulties and it has not been fully carried out. The biggest reason is that the scope specified for the work in the past was too complex and too detailed, making it easy to lose focus and reducing efficiency. The key points decided at this training conference are, on the one hand, to concentrate talent and strength, and on the other hand, for the future work policy, the Central Government will only provide the outlines and use new training methods to unify the will of the nation. The trivial matters will be handled by lower-level agencies in accordance with the circumstances, so that there is room for activity, which will be sufficient to facilitate progress. (2) The capital construction is not a local problem in Nanjing, but an overall national problem. Everyone should have a concept of national construction and bear it together with full force, so that it can be carried out step by step. However, all localities only know about the provinces and cities, and have not paid attention to the nation, so that the construction of the capital has lacked a grand plan for two years. In the future, propaganda should be widely disseminated to promote respect for the capital in all directions, to understand the importance of construction, and to cooperate in its progress. (3) The Second National Education Conference is a major key to improving education in the future. The advantage of the plan set at the First National Education Conference is that the declaration of the conference to implement the Three Principles of the People's Education is in line with modern trends and is not limited by old Confucian prejudices. The disadvantage is that most of the various proposals are empty, and very few practical main measures are specified. This conference is based on the education policies set by the Fourth and Fifth Plenary Sessions of the Second Central Committee and the Third National Congress, and uses the plan of the First National Education Conference as a reference. I believe that most of the participants are famous figures in the education field, and they will certainly be able to make magnificent plans and create a systematic law to open a new era for education and establish a fundamental plan for the country. (4) Regarding the National Games, 21 units of provinces, cities, and overseas Chinese groups participated. The rapid progress of the results is enough to create a new record in the history of Chinese sports. Compared with the results of the World Games, it is still inevitably behind. In the future, we should continue to strive for excellence, so that the next National Games will have even more outstanding achievements. All the referees of this conference were Chinese, and no foreigners participated, and representatives and athletes from all sides were able to obey consistently, which is a good phenomenon. (5) The purpose of holding the Boy Scout General Review is to concentrate the spirit of each group, complete the organization, popularize the training, increase experience, and develop skills. It can also make the people of the whole country pay attention to military and national education, know what to observe and feel, and be determined to revitalize it. It is also a major manifestation of the party's training work. As for the comrades working in the Central Government, I have proposed that the Central Party Headquarters open a sports field and set up a library and club to exercise their bodies, increase their talents, and liven up their spirits. I hope this matter can be realized as soon as possible. The meeting adjourned after the report.

▲National Government: At 10 AM on the same morning, the National Government held the Sun Yat-sen Memorial Week. Over three hundred people attended, including Chiang Kai-shek, Tan Yankai, Wang Chonghui, Gu Yingfen, Zhu Peide, Wu Siyu, Chen Yi, Yang Jie, Lin Xiang, Wei Daoming, Zhu Luhe, Liu Ruiheng, Wang Zhengting, Zhang Wohua, Li Jinlun, Enhe Batu, Shao Yuanchong, Li Zhonggong, Jiao Yitang, and officials from the National Government's civil and military affairs departments. Chiang Kai-shek chaired the meeting and gave the following political report: "Comrades, there have been no major changes in the military situation in the past week. It is said that Feng Yuxiang arrived in Zhengzhou the day before yesterday. Yan Xishan sent Xu Yongchang and Yang Aiyuan to Zhengzhou to meet with Feng to discuss military plans. It is reported that Yan Xishan has not issued a single cent of the military expenses promised to the various armies for the past month, except for giving Feng Yuxiang 500,000 yuan. Therefore, the various armies will naturally resent Yan's favoritism. However, Yan Xishan still wants them to attack the Central Government. We also hope that they will attack, so that they can throw themselves into the net and the military situation can be quickly concluded. Because if they do not attack, the military situation will be prolonged by one day, which is one more day of suffering for the people. Now we not only have enough defense, but also have preparations to wipe them out in one fell swoop. There are currently no major problems in the Zhengzhou area. As for Laohekou, Junxian, and Yunyang in northern Hubei, all the Northwest Army has been completely wiped out, but the newspapers in Tianjin and Beijing are arbitrarily spreading rumors, saying that Laohekou and other places have been occupied by them. In fact, they are trying to deceive Yan Xishan. They also say that Sun Dianying has contacted the Central Government's Third Division, and that the Third Division has failed. This is completely slander. In fact, the sentries of the two sides are still hundreds of miles apart. They are just exaggerating one more time to ask Yan Xishan for more money. Now the rift between Yan and Feng is growing day by day, and they are deceiving each other. Feng said that the Northwest Army has arrived in Zhengzhou, but in fact, most of them are still in Xi'an, trying to attack Taiyuan. These facts have already clearly told us that Yan and Feng will soon split. As for the reorganizationists and the Western Hills faction being unable to cooperate, that is also what we expected. Now we just need to concentrate on rectifying the interior and wait for them to attack. Regarding the political aspect, our government colleagues feel that they cannot measure whether they are progressing or regressing, but when we look back at what we have done in the past month, we have made progress compared to the past. In terms of the National Movement, the National Games have been held and have achieved very good results. The results of the National Boy Scout Review have also been unprecedented. Now the National Education Conference is being held, and there are more practical proposals being carried out. Such achievements have not been made in a single month since the beginning of the Republic of China. From this, on the one hand, the spirit of the people can be expressed, and on the other hand, it is also political progress. This matter has a huge impact, increasing our spirit several times, which is greater than any power. When foreigners see that the warlords on the other side are acting so recklessly, while we are working so hard on construction, it also shocks them. We can be very gratified in our hearts about this. It can be seen that everything is more organized and orderly than before, and the foundation of the revolution is gradually being consolidated. In terms of diplomacy, there has been much progress recently. The treaty for the recovery of Weihaiwei has been signed. Most countries have signed the autonomous tariff treaty, except for Japan. Now the Japanese Privy Council has passed it, and it should be signed soon. In this light, our hope for tariff autonomy has been completely realized. After this goal is achieved, the national economic foundation will naturally be consolidated, and the national economy will inevitably develop accordingly. Therefore, although the reactionaries are trying their best to slander the Central Government, saying that it cannot abolish the unequal treaties, now it seems that we can abolish the unequal treaties. No matter how the reactionaries spread rumors, they cannot erase the facts. We believe that if all comrades and the people of the whole country work together, and the government can do things step by step, the independence of China can certainly be achieved. Therefore, for the revolution, the rebellion of Yan and Feng has instead increased our infinite strength and courage. We feel very optimistic about the future of the revolution. In addition, there are a few words that I have long wanted to say to you, the newspaper reporters, but I have not had a suitable opportunity. The last time I reviewed the troops in Shanghai, I said to Commander Xiong that regarding the censorship of news, there is no need to delete a paragraph or a word from what is published in the newspapers, as long as they do not publish military actions. Therefore, recently all news has been allowed to be published by the newspapers, so it is inevitable that there will be inaccuracies, especially in what is published in the Shishi Xinbao. Newspapers are originally intended to lead the people and be national teachers, especially for political matters, they must be careful when publishing. Often, the news obtained by reporters has not been verified, and they use it to attack others in the hope of raising their own status. This is not the attitude that newspaper reporters should have. Therefore, many party members are dissatisfied with the attitude of several newspapers in Shanghai recently, because now the people of the whole country clearly recognize the Central Government and the rebels, but the Shanghai newspapers mostly publish news from the north in the front of the newspaper, while news from the Central Government is placed in the back. Who are the rebels, who are the revolutionaries, what is right and wrong, and what is true and false are not distinguished. If the journalistic community is so unclear about right and wrong, what value does it have? How the newspapers publish is absolutely not interfered with by the government, but the news must be accurate. Usually, the opinions of the newspapers do not matter much, but in this critical period, to attack the government for no reason is to be regarded as reactionary speech and speech that aids the rebels. If the journalistic community cannot distinguish between right and wrong, it cannot be free. I hope that newspaper reporters will pay attention. In the future, reporters can freely express their opinions except on military matters, but they must not attack the government with one or two inaccurate words to increase the power of the reactionaries. If they criticize the government, as long as it is factual and justified, that is what they should do; otherwise, they are aiding the rebels. What is the difference between a newspaper that aids the rebels and an army that aids the rebels? I will be going to Wuhan for a review in a few days, and I should be back in Nanjing in about one or two weeks. During this time, I hope that everyone will work harder to make full preparations in all political and economic aspects so that we can resolve the situation with swift means. This is what I deeply hope for."

Bandits Rampant Near Jiaozhou Bay

▲ Qingdao Police and Warships Rushed to Suppress Them

▲ Bandits Fled to Jiaojing After Looting Lingshanwei

Qingdao Correspondence: The area around Dazhu Mountain and Xiaozhu Mountain near Jiaozhou Bay has long been a den of bandits. Recently, bandit leaders Wang Zicheng and Li Xiaoqi and others have gathered their followers and established strongholds, engaging in robbery from time to time. These bandits have about 500 followers and more than 200 rifles. They are recruiting vagrants and their ambitions are not small. In addition to robbing in Jiaoxian County, Wang Zicheng's gang recently invaded the Qingdao municipal jurisdiction. The Municipal Public Security Bureau reported that Haixi is close to Qingdao and its security is of great importance to Qingdao and Jiaozhou Bay. The Third Branch Bureau Chief Chen was dispatched a few days ago, leading more than 100 police officers and security team members, together with the Haixi garrison police, to take the "Flying Whale" small steamer to suppress the bandits. The Northeast Naval Headquarters also dispatched the warship "Yongxiang" with a detachment of marines to assist in suppressing the bandits south of Dazhu Mountain. Hearing the news, the bandits fled from Xuejiadao (Qingdao City) to Lingshanwei to avoid conflict with the military and police. After arriving in Lingshanwei, they looted the entire town and kidnapped more than 30 people, fleeing northwest. Lingshanwei is a major town in Jiaonan, with developed commerce and a reputation for prosperity. After this tragic robbery, its vitality has been greatly damaged. The Qingdao police and navy, because the bandits had fled the Qingdao municipal jurisdiction, have reorganized and returned to Qingdao. (April 19)

Jinan City Area Delineated

Jinan Correspondence: Jinan was changed to a city last May when the provincial government moved to Jinan. Regarding the city area issue, the municipal government advocated expansion to protect the city's security. Licheng County, however, believed that the city area was too large, and the county area would inevitably shrink. The county government and various agencies rose up to argue, and several meetings were held in the municipal government without a resolution. Mayor Zhao Jingshi then submitted the reasons for the necessary expansion of the city area to the Department of Civil Affairs for referral to the provincial government for review. The provincial government's standing committee resolved to appoint members such as Yu Enbo to review the matter. The results of the review were reported to the provincial government. Yesterday, the provincial government's 80th committee meeting approved the review plan. The city area is approximately 30 li long in each direction, east, west, north, and south. The boundary lines of its jurisdiction are as follows: (1) The eastern boundary line extends from Xiaojie, passing through Hongjiayuan, Taipingzhuang, Bajianpu, Xianjianzhuang, and Xiheling, to Laoshigou. (2) The southern boundary line extends from Foyulongdong, passing through Daling Xinglongzhuang, and Fenshuiling, to Wenzhuang. (3) The western boundary line extends from Huangshangling, passing through Renjiashankou, Dayangjiazhuang, Yinmazhuang, and Xishawangzhuang, to Luzhuang. (4) The northern boundary line is the Yellow River. (19th)

Xie Bin's Troops May Be Resolved Peacefully

▲ Representatives Sent to Apologize and Seek Peace

▲ He Jian Orders Them to Go to Western Hubei

▲ The Disaster of War in Western Hunan Has Been Fortunately Avoided

Changsha Correspondence: Since the assassination of Chen Hanzhang, the commander of the Independent Eighth Brigade, the Li Guojun Regiment of the brigade took the opportunity to mutiny and engaged in war with the Chen Wo Department, the acting Brigade Commander. The newly formed 10th Division, Xie Bin's Department, immediately advanced from Tianzhu, Guizhou, and stationed in Hunan to assist the Li Regiment in attacking the Chen Department. They fought across the river in Qianyang for nine days and nights. Chen Wo's troops were weak and only defended Qianyang City to protect themselves, resulting in the occupation of Hongjiang and a serious situation. He Jian repeatedly telegraphed urging them to leave the province, but Xie and others ignored him. He then decided on a large-scale suppression plan, in addition to telegraphing Mao Guangxiang, Chairman of Guizhou Province, to send Wang Jialie's troops into Hunan to assist in the suppression, he also recalled the Peng Weiren Brigade, and also dispatched a regiment each from Dai Douyuan's Chen Quzhen Department, and He Jian's Li Xuan Regiment, as rebel suppression troops, with Luo Fanying, commander of the 16th Division, as commander. Luo had returned to Changsha from Quanzhou on the 15th, and telegraphed the Peng Brigade and Li Regiment to concentrate in Wugang Baoqing, awaiting orders to advance. Luo himself was scheduled to go to Bao from the province on the 18th to arrange everything. The war clouds in western Hunan momentarily filled the air. Xie Bin, Li Guojun and others were quite alarmed upon hearing this news. Also, because they had been attacking Qianyang for a long time without success, and Mao of Qianyang had sent Deputy Brigade Commander Deng Zhiting to lead the Hou and Liu Regiments to attack them from both sides in Hunan, Chen Wo took the opportunity to counterattack, and Li Guojun suffered heavy losses. Therefore, on the 14th, they abandoned Hongjiang, and also lifted the siege of Qianyang, and retreated to Zhijiang for a meeting. Knowing that the future was difficult to achieve, they sent representatives to Hongjiang to express their willingness to make peace, and telegraphed the province to explain the misunderstanding, and requested instructions on the route to Hubei. At this point, the military situation between Hunan and Guizhou has a hope of reconciliation. Here are two telegrams from Chen Wo and Xiang Chengzu, the senator who went to Hongjiang to investigate, (Telegram 1) Report of Victory, 1. According to a telegram from Hongjiang, the rebels from Qianyang City crossed the river at dawn, and were severely attacked by our troops head-on, sinking two rebel ships, killing rebel Battalion Commander Li Guojun and dozens of officers and soldiers. At that time, the Hou and Liu Regiments of Mao's troops in Qianyang also provided assistance from the front, and the rebels were greatly defeated and fled in disarray. Our brigade headquarters has now advanced to Ganxiping. 2. Chen Dongsheng (Wo) led his troops and the local defense entered Hong on the cold day, and the Liu Zhuming (Xie Bin Regiment Commander) rebel troops retreated to Ruoshui. The brothers are allowed to go to Hong on the Xiao day. Your brother Xiang Chengzu respectfully deletes the Hai seal, (Telegram 2) The Li rebels colluded with two regiments of the Xie Division, and attacked Qian in separate ways. After the official supervised the team to stop them, from the slight beginning to the cold end, fortunately the troops of Mao's department in Qianyang went to the rescue, and the soldiers used their lives. The Battle of Niutoushan was enough to frighten the enemy. Because Xie felt that it was difficult to violate the great righteousness, he specially sent a representative, Li Jianzhong, to come to apologize and seek peace, and promised to move to western Hubei immediately, and said that he had strictly investigated the troublemaking regiments. Now a part of the army has retreated to Yuanzhou (that is, Zhijiang) City, and Li rebels are stationed outside the city. A part retreated to Huitong, and our army is tracking and pursuing. On the Zhijiang side, it has reached Tiedunpo, and on the Huitong side, it is also making progress. May I ask if you can specify the route and order Xie's troops to move to western Hubei, and wait for instructions. I respectfully telegraph this report, Chen Wo respectfully bows the Xian Wu seal.

He Jian believed that since Xie had agreed to go to western Hubei, there would be no problem. He immediately replied to Xie with a telegram, ordering him to leave Hunan according to the specified route. The text said, "Urgent, Commander Xie Xun of Chenzhou and Yuanzhou, sent by Tan, each telegram has been read, the Chen Brigade and Li Regiment rebelled, and are being investigated and dealt with. The Liu Regiment of your department helped the rebels to make trouble, and repeatedly occupied Hongjiang, and has repeatedly reported to Commander-in-Chief Chiang and Chief Supervisor He to stop it. Yesterday, Regiment Commander Zhu Ming of Liu sent a telegram from Hongjiang saying that Zhu Ming was ordered to go to Hubei and came to Hong by the way, and asked the Chen Brigade to withdraw quickly, and as soon as the Qianbian merchants arrive in Hong, they will continue to advance, etc. It has been confirmed that the 55th and 56th Regiments of your department are stationed in Hongjiang and Denglong Bridge and Baima Pavilion across the river from Qianyang, and have been attacking the Chen Brigade for days, and Acting Brigade Commander Chen has been besieged. It is obvious that he intends to help the rebels. There is no reason for a revolutionary to take a stand. According to the previous telegram, you should immediately go through Zhijiang, Mayang, Qiancheng, and Yongshun, and quickly open to western Hubei to maintain the prestige of the central government, otherwise, for the sake of the security of Hunan Province, it will also be detrimental to your department. Especially reply, your brother He Jian bows", At the same time, Chen Chen Quzhen was notified by telegram that Xie's troops were allowed to take the Maqian Yong route to Hubei, and to monitor their departure from the country properly. Therefore, Luo Fanying's trip to Bao has also been postponed.

Longyan Communist Bandits Re-Occupy Xipuying

▲ Zhan Diaoyuan's Family Kidnapped

Xiamen Correspondence, 19th: Since Longyan organized the Western Fujian Soviet, the flames of communism in Western Fujian have been rekindled. After the communist leader Deng Zihui led 2,000 bandits to capture Yongfu, the Zhangzhou garrison was heavily guarded in Nan Jing and Huaan, and they did not dare to go south. They then fled eastward, sending their false second Regiment Commander Deng Gangyi to lead more than 1,000 bandits to spy on Zhangping. They captured Yuntan Town on the 15th. The local militia Chen Naiwu was outnumbered and had dozens of firearms seized. Liu Liebo retreated to the Liancheng border. After Yuntan was captured, Xipuying was in imminent danger. Xipuying is an important town in eastern Longyan, connected to Zhangping. After Yuntan was captured, Liu Liebo and others all retreated first, leaving only 60 or 70 men from the local militia Zhan Jifu's Department. Zhan is the younger brother of the provincial commissioner Zhan Diaoyuan and a prominent local family. Knowing that the situation was critical, they were on guard day and night. From the 6th to the 13th, there was no movement. At dawn on the 14th, Deng Gangyi suddenly led 1,000 bandits to attack, surrounding Xipuying. They first disarmed the militia sentries, then broke into the fortified buildings, and kidnapped all the militiamen and able-bodied men, women and children of the Zhan family inside the buildings, totaling more than 30 members of Zhan Diaoyuan's family. Zhan Jifu was also among them. The Zhan family's fortified building, named Jinmin, was built in the late Ming Dynasty and could accommodate 400 people. It was the largest fortress in Xipuying. After the bandits broke into the building, they looted all the property and set fire to the building. There was also Zhan Bi, a wealthy man in Xipuying, with more than 100,000 yuan in assets, who was also kidnapped and taken to Longyan. Xipuying is the richest area in eastern Longyan, 20 li from Yuntan and 20 li from Zhangpu County. This capture was more devastating than the loss of Yongfu Baisha, with approximately 80 firearms lost. After Xipuying was captured, communist bandits were also spotted as sentries in Jitai, 60 li from Zhangping. There is no garrison in Zhangping, only Chen Guohua and Lin Weibang's security team of one or two hundred men. Hearing the news, they did not dare to defend the city and retreated to Heshun Township, 20 li from the city. Stores in the city have been closed, and those with a little property have fled to Zhangzhou. The newly formed 1st Division stationed in Zhangzhou heard that it would transfer a battalion of Huang's Regiment from the Huaan garrison to assist, but Huaan is close to Yongfu, and the defense is also very tight, so it is not known whether it can be transferred.

Xiamen Convenience Steamer Sinking Case

▲ Tong'an County Has Interrogated Relevant Personnel Once

Xiamen Correspondence: After the "Convenience" steamer sank, the ship's crew was unharmed. Except for the helmsman Su Qili, who escaped, the engineer Huang Dianzhong and the sailors Li Shuishi and Xu Renyu were all arrested by the Wudian Tong'an Public Security Bureau Branch and sent to the Tong'an County Government. A court hearing has been held, and their testimonies are as follows: Li Shuishi testified that he is from Hui'an, 24 years old, and works as a sailor and cook on the "Convenience" motorboat for a monthly salary of 14 yuan. He has been on the ship for six or seven months. The ship usually carries about 120 passengers, most of whom buy connecting tickets from Shuitou to Meiren Palace. Wang Antong from Oucuo sells tickets at sea. He runs the Kaiyuanli grocery store in Aotou. The helmsman Su Qili is from Aotou. There are six people on the ship. Wang Antong takes care of the affairs on the ship. If Wang is not on the ship, the helmsman Su Qili is in charge. The motorboat was bought from Taiwan by the Quanmu Company in Xiamen and is four or five years old. This time, the sailors explained to the stationmaster of Wang Antong station that the ship body was damaged and needed to be repaired. The stationmaster, named Bao Ying but the surname is unknown, said that the Xiujiang motorboat repair was not finished and had to run. There are two motorboats running in this place, one is Xiujiang, which is under repair, leaving only the Convenience. On this day, it sailed from Aotou to Banyuan, and the wind and waves were too large, and it was激沉没. Wang Antong was not on the ship this time, Su Qili was on the ship, and his life and death are unpredictable. It is also said that the old chief inspector of Quan He Company, Lin Tianshou, the new chief inspector, is a Cantonese whose surname is unknown. Xu Renyu testified that he is from Dadeng, Jinmen County, 23 years old, and has parents at home. He joined the ship on the tenth day of the second month of the lunar calendar this year, working as a sailor for a monthly salary of 14 yuan, the same as Li Shuishi. The number of passengers carried at Aotou is notified to the Wutong Station by raising a flag, and the car is sent to pick them up. This time, the sailors notified the stationmaster Bao Ying of the Wutong Station that the ship body was damaged and needed to be repaired. According to the station, only this ship is left and must be run. Wang Antong is on board to take care of the affairs of the ship at sea, and the salary and foreign water is about sixty or seventy yuan per month. The old manager of Quan He Company's surname is Huang. This time, the new manager Chen Youcai was replaced. The previous chief inspector, Lin Tianshou, was familiar with the situation. The new chief inspector is not skilled, causing the ship to have broken spaces, overload, water flooded into the ship, unable to pump water, passengers panicked, and the ship tilted and sank. The ocean from Aotou to Wutong is about ten miles, and it takes half an hour to drive. The ship sailed at half past four o'clock, and it sank at about five o'clock. The Convenience ship has been damaged for more than ten days. Because the Xiujiang motorboat repair has not been completed, the rest of the testimony is the same as Li Shuishi's. Huang Dianzhong testified that he is from Nankang, Minhou, 25 years old, and joined the ship in September of the lunar calendar last year, serving as a driver for a monthly salary of 35 yuan. The ship was bought from Taiwan four or five years ago, and the machine is not damaged. The ship body has leaks. At that time, the customs signed the name, and only 85 passengers were allowed. This time, there were about 100 passengers. Wang Antong was not on the ship and opened the Kaiyuanli grocery store in Aotou. This time the ship leaked, and everyone has notified Bao Ying. According to the answer, the Xiujiang is not finished repairing and must drive. This time there were too many passengers, the wind and waves were too big, the water flooded into the boat, causing it to sink. The rest of the testimony is the same as Li Shuishi and Xu Renyu. Qiu Jun, the county magistrate of Tong'an, believed that the case was of great importance, so he sent a commissioner Ge Minghao on the 16th with three official letters, one to the Siming County Government, one to the Xiamen Maritime Public Security Bureau, and one to the Siming District Court, to discuss the handling of the case. Deng Jian, President of the Siming District Court, believed that the incident occurred in the jurisdiction of Tong'an, and should be handled by Tong'an County. The Tong'an County Magistrate believed that the defendant, Jinhe Company's Automobile Company, was located in the Siming County border, and should be jointly tried by the judicial authorities of the two counties in a special court. However, the Procuratorate of the Siming District Court believed that most of the parties involved were under its jurisdiction and could not be ignored. Therefore, on the 16th, the relatives of the victims Fang Tianxi, Fang Youzhi, Fang Fuquan, and Fang Fulian, and the defendant, Chen, the manager of Quanhe Automobile Company, were summoned to court for questioning. The defendant did not arrive. The trial was resumed on the 17th, and the defendant still did not appear. An arrest warrant has now been issued.

▲ Director of the Special Education Department Replaced

Harbin Correspondence, 15th: After the "International Coordination News" was smashed, the activities of the Communist Party in Harbin received extreme attention from the Northeast authorities. Liao Fang had received a secret report that, in addition to Wang Lifeng and Yu Ergui, the other major communist leaders were Dai Haizhou and Zhang Baosi. Zhang Baosi was arrested, and Wang Lifeng and Yu Ergui had fled without a trace. Dai Haizhou was hiding in the port, moving several times a day, secretly plotting to incite a strike among the 36 shed railway workers. On the 10th of this month, the Northeast Political Affairs Committee telegraphed the Special Police Department, setting a deadline of three days to arrest Dai and send him to Liaoning. Bao Wenyou, director of the Special Police Department, secretly ordered the detective team, the investigation bureau, and the heads of each department to arrest Dai within three days and offered a reward of 1,000 yuan. Yesterday, the 14th, the detective team leader Zhu Baoshan discovered that Dai was hiding in the home of a Russian in Qinjiagang West Ba Zha City. At 9:00 PM that night, he led several police officers to arrest him and found a work plan on his body, which detailed the plan to carry out agitation of the labor movement and burn down important government offices. After being arrested, he was interrogated overnight and sent to Liaoning at 10:40 PM on the 15th. The police feared that his accomplices would gather to make trouble, so they forbade the newspapers from publishing this news. The newspapers' defense against the Communist Party has not yet been lifted. Printing factories are equipped with wooden sticks and iron pestles for use in the event of an attack by thugs. There are quite a few dangerous elements among the students of secondary schools in the Special Zone. Recently, they have also organized groups such as the Anti-Imperialist Great Alliance and the Freedom Alliance, sending declarations to the newspapers and forcing them to publish them. The newspapers have all refused. These people have threatened to destroy all the newspapers in the port and burn them down in the next few days, and have organized a suicide squad to attack the newspaper factories. Therefore, the police authorities ordered the security team to be dispatched day and night to prevent any unexpected events. The Liao authorities believed that the thinking of students in the special zone was deteriorating day by day, and decided to take the opportunity to actively eliminate it before it spread. Therefore, they specially transferred Zhang Guozhen, the director of the Department of Education, back to the Border Defense Commander's Office to serve as a secretary, and sent another capable person to Harbin to rectify it. However, it has not yet been announced. It is heard that the Third International's Red Internationalization of the Northeast has already planned the steps. The first step is to use money to buy Chinese youths who are not determined and carry out a terrorist plan. Therefore, the authorities are strictly preventing it and are also trying their best to be thorough.

Local Correspondence

Songjiang

Li Xinglin and Others' Kidnapping Account: Regarding the case of Zhangyan Town being robbed and kidnapped by bandits, Mr. Li and others came to Song yesterday to recount their experiences of being kidnapped. Li said that after being kidnapped on the evening of the 1st, there were a total of 14 bandit ships. All the victims were loaded onto the bandit ships. The next morning, they arrived at the Guanwang Temple near Zhujiage. The bandit leader then ordered sentries to be dispatched on the land and water routes to stop passing merchants. At the same time, he interrogated the hostages at the Guanwang Temple. Seeing those who looked poor, he ordered them to board the hijacked Shanghai-Zhangyan bus and sent them back to Zhangyan. The rest, except for the owner of the porcelain shop, who was immediately shot, were driven into seven bandit ships. Smokers were given opium. Most of the two meals in the afternoon and evening were served with ham. They traveled all the way, stopping at towns. It was not until the 6th that they encountered the water police. The sound of gunfire was constant throughout the day and did not stop until late at night. Five bandit ships lost track of the others in the middle of the night. At noon on the 12th, they encountered Li Jingcheng's water police unit in Bacheng, and two companies of the army from Kunshan surrounded the bandit ships and killed more than 40 bandits. The 20 or so of us who were victimized were completely rescued and are grateful for our new lives.

Fengjing Captures Kidnappers: Because there are kidnappers and hostages hiding near Fengjing, they have now been captured by the town's Public Security Bureau and Security Corps. It is heard that there are two women and two bandits. They are scheduled to be reported to Songjiang for interrogation on the 22nd.

Jiading

Preliminary Trial Record of the Fire Wine Case: Zhou Zhenxin Winery, newly opened outside the West Gate, was reported by six of its peers, including Jin Boqin, the manager of Huiji, and others, for selling fire wine mixed with water, which is detrimental to public health. Zhu, director of the County Public Security Bureau, led detectives and also met with the original reporter to search. Seven altars of fire wine were found in the store, and seven altars of fire wine were found in the home of the owner Zhou Weixin, as well as a large number of untaxed yellow wine. The wine altars and Zhou Zialeng were taken to the county together. Later, the Tobacco and Wine Monopoly Bureau issued a certificate that the yellow wine was not tax-evaded, and A Leng was temporarily released on bail. As for whether the fire wine is true, the county government summoned representatives of various agencies to open the altars on the spot, take samples, and send them to Shanghai for expert testing. Zhou Weixin filed a lawsuit with the county government, saying that he lost clothing and other items when his bedroom was searched, accusing Jin and others of theft. The county trial officer opened a preliminary trial on the afternoon of the 19th. The plaintiff Zhou Aleng slightly supplied, I was on the 塲 at the beginning of the search, and later the family members all escaped, only one worker was at home, etc., and the hall said that the wine test fee was about one hundred yuan, and you should be responsible for it. The plaintiff said that it was not fire wine, and they were nosy, and the testing fee should not be borne by me. Jin Boqin, Zhao, Han and other six people were questioned in the second 訉, and slightly supplied that we went together because Director Zhu wanted us to help check the fire wine, but Aleng accompanied us during the search and did not enter his bedroom, etc. Jin Boqin said that I am the director of the Kuanchan Department, the chairman of the Yicang Committee, and the executive chairman of the County Chamber of Commerce. Now I am falsely accused of robbery and should be counter-sued according to the law. The hall ordered a change of date for another trial.

Suzhou

Water Police Organize Patrol Team: Gong, the district chief of the third district of the water public security, believed that the bandits in Yangcheng Lake had been wiped out, so yesterday (21st) he ordered the teams to transfer several patrol boats to form a patrol team, which was dispatched by Chu Boying, the captain of the eleventh team, to deal with patrolling the Yangcheng Lake area to search for bandit tracks. In addition, Li Guozhen, the captain of the twelfth team, presented to District Chief Gong yesterday, saying that the bandits in Yangcheng Lake have been wiped out, and asked to withdraw the road patrol boats back to their original defense.

Suspected Bandit Carrying Money to Buy Guns Caught: Zhang Lesan, a patrol officer of the eighth branch, discovered a suspicious person outside the Panmen Wulong Bridge the night before last and questioned him. According to him, he came to Suzhou from his hometown and took a boat. There were two bandits on the boat who were sleeping soundly, so I escaped ashore and found banknotes worth 1,017 yuan next to the man. Patrol Officer Zhang questioned him repeatedly, and he finally said that his name was Chen Taichang, and the money was ordered by the bandit leader Fei to come to Suzhou to buy a handgun. Patrol Officer Zhang suspected that Chen was very suspicious, so he took the suspect to the station and sent him to the Municipal Public Security Bureau yesterday. Now the bandit suppression headquarters has sent a letter to the Municipal Bureau for consultation, and it has replied that Chen claims to be a hostage.

Court Asks to Increase Prison Expenses: Wei Bangzhen, the chief secretary of the High Court, went to Beijing on the 19th to present to the Ministry of Justice and Administration, requesting an increase in the expenses of the new and old prisons in each county to maintain the lives of the guards, etc. Minister Wei received him and replied that he would plan for it immediately and send a letter to the provincial government ordering the Department of Finance to review it.

Wuxi

Detailed Record of the German Inspection Group's Arrival in Wuxi for Investigation: The German industrial inspection group came to China to investigate industries. They arrived in Wuxi by express train from Zhenjiang at 9:00 PM the day before yesterday (the 19th). The county magistrate of this county, Sun Daoshi, the chief of the Public Security Bureau, Huang Zhenbai, industrialists Rong Desheng, Rong Ersheng, Cai Jiansan, and dozens of others went to the station to welcome them. After the group members got off the train, they were led to the Washington Hotel by the welcoming party. In addition to the ten German industrialists such as Mr. Leitzmann, the members of the National Government reception committee also accompanied them to Wuxi. After the group members arrived at the Washington Hotel, the reporter went to pay his respects. Soon, the secretary-general of the group, Mr. Shi Dewei, came out to talk and said that in order to seek the development of industry, it is necessary to pay attention to scientization, and then the production can be expected to increase dramatically. Germany has been able to use scientization to promote industrial development. At this juncture, China is also planning construction. In recent years, it has also felt an upward trend in industry. My colleagues have long admired the developed factories and the great development of industry in your county. Combined with the beauty of the mountains and rivers, they have long wanted to come and visit. Now that they have fulfilled their wish, they are very gratified, etc. The reporter then said goodbye and left. Yesterday, at about 10:00 AM on the 28th, various agencies and industrialists Rong Desheng, etc., accompanied the group to visit the Guangqin Qingfeng Yukang three yarn factories and the Gansheng silk factory Shenxin yarn factory. The group members greatly appreciated the improvement of the machinery and the excellence of the products of the above factories. In the afternoon, they took a steamboat to Meiyuan, Taihu Lake, Yuantouzhu and other places for sightseeing. They stayed at the Taihu Hotel that night. This morning (21st), they went to visit the Yongtai Minfeng Zhenyi three silk factories and flour mills outside the South Gate. In the afternoon, they took a car back to Shanghai.

A Murder Case Due to Jealousy Outside the West Gate: Shi Fuquan, the owner of the Xinchang shoe store under the shed outside the West Gate of this county, is from Jiangbei. He had an affair with Wu Liu, a female worker in the Shenxin No. 3 Factory, for three years. They lived together like a couple. Recently, Fuquan heard that Wu Liu had a new love. He was so jealous that he hid a sharp scissors the night before last at about 8:00 PM and tricked Wu Liu to an deserted area behind the West Xinlou. Without asking for the reason, he stabbed Wu Liu's head indiscriminately with the scissors. Liu cried out for help and resisted with all her might, causing stab wounds to her neck and hands. Seeing that he had caused a disaster, Shi took out a match and sorghum wine from his bag and swallowed them together in an attempt to commit suicide. The patrol police Zhao Yucheng of the Fourth Branch of the Public Security Bureau took the murderer Shi Fuquan, the injured Wu Liu, and a pair of scissors to the County Public Security Bureau for interrogation. He ordered Shi Fuquan to be sent to the Labor Hospital for treatment, and Wu Liu was temporarily detained for further investigation.

Thieves Arrested and Sent to the County for Interrogation: Mao Mujun, the captain of the second district of the Water Police Team stationed in Wuxi, arrested six thieves including Zheng Shiying, Xue Apen, Wang Ada, Zhang Ayi, Zheng Shikuan, and Chen Sheng Gu on the 16th of this month and sent them to the county for interrogation yesterday afternoon. Zheng Shiying confessed that he robbed a big pig boat at Lvjiangkou and stole twenty-nine big pigs, and also robbed more than twenty dan of white rice from a certain family in Huayuannong, as well as clothes and silver ornaments from the south gate of the Water Immortal Temple, Dongfeng Ditianxia, Wumuzhen and other places, and did not deny sharing the spoils and spending them. The other five thieves, Xue Apen and others, all confessed to robbery, etc. Zhou Cheng, the trial judge, immediately ordered them to be detained together and wait for verification and judgment based on their confessions.

Qingguo Lane Robbery Case: Wu Yuchang Distillery in Qingguo Lane in the city of this county, at 11:00 PM last night, was settling accounts and closing the market, when two robbers suddenly came, wearing long black cloth shirts and speaking with a strong Jiangbei accent. One robber was guarding outside the door, and the other went straight into the counter, pulled out a pistol, and scared everyone into silence. The robber then robbed 111 yuan in silver dollars, 110 jiao in small dollars, and 19 jiao in silver dollar notes from the iron box. After the robbery, the two robbers fled towards the South Gate.

Paper Transport Boat Robbed on Taihu Lake: Sun Meiji, a paper merchant from outside the South Gate of this county, fully loaded his paper cargo from Hangzhou the day before yesterday and set sail for Wuxi. When passing near Manshan in Taihu Lake, he suddenly encountered two pirate ships. More than twenty pirates jumped out with weapons and crowded onto the boat to search. It was estimated that they robbed more than fifty yuan in cash, fifty yuan in drafts, six partner bedding, as well as clothes, rice, oil and other items, worth more than 300 yuan. After the pirates got the loot, they left in a boat and went away.

Japanese Industrialists Arrive for Inspection: Nagata Akira of the Japanese Toa Company and Misawa Tanemi of the Chiba Store, both industrialists of the group, came to Wuxi by train the day before yesterday to inspect the current situation of the silk cocoon industry, as Wuxi is the center of China's silk cocoon industry. Tomorrow, they will go to Dingchang, Changyongtai and other silk factories for detailed inspection.

Arrest and Investigate Obstruction of Conscription and Road Construction: Conscription and road construction on the Xichang Provincial Road began on the 18th. However, the public in various places along the road line generally criticized that the new road line ran through the fields, so they all adopted a wait-and-see attitude. When the Construction Bureau sent personnel to spread gray marks near Anzhen the day before yesterday, the villagers saw many people trampling in the wheat fields outside the line, causing a lot of damage, so they complained, resulting in a conflict. As a result, the villagers, Ni Afu, were identified as deliberately obstructing the construction, and Mao Fengming, the director of the sub-office, reported to the county government to detain Ni Afu and send him to the county government for interrogation.

Changzhou

A Changxing Sian Ship Robbed on Taihu Lake: A ship sailing from Changzhou to Changxing Sian, passed near Jiaoshan in Taihu Lake at 11:00 AM on the 18th, and suddenly encountered a pirate ship, which ordered it to stop and fired a gun as a demonstration. More than twenty pirates swarmed onto the ship and stabbed the ship's manager Wang Xida and the ship's mate Yang Pan Gen in several places with knives, causing serious injuries. The goods and other items on the ship were all robbed. The total loss was estimated to be more than 700 yuan. Afterwards, the ship sailed back to Changzhou and carried the injured to the Xijiao Hospital for treatment.

Meeting of the Grain Storage Management Committee: The Wu Yi Grain Storage Management Committee held a meeting at 3:00 PM on the 20th to discuss matters: (1) The problem of relieving the people's food. It was resolved to ask the merchants to convene rice merchants to plan specific methods to purchase a large amount of grain for relief. (2) The exact amount of grain and grain money stored in the former Huainan and other ten townships has not been reported. It is proposed to ask the district chiefs of the relevant districts to help investigate the case. It was resolved to send letters to the district chiefs of districts 1, 2, 3, 4, 7, and 10, stipulating a date, to convene the original managers of the city and township to hold a meeting to check the exact amount, and notify the committee to send personnel to attend.

Communist Disturbance, Citywide Panic: In the Dongjie Shanmen Lane area of Tongcheng, more than ten Communists caused a disturbance at about 8:00 PM on the 19th, and dispersed after more than ten minutes, distributing leaflets and shouting slogans. At that time, the whole city was in a panic, and stores closed one after another. When the police arrived, the Communists had all fled.

Auditing Bandit Suppression Expenses: The funds used for suppressing the Pan bandits in Tongyi last year will be audited and announced by representatives from all walks of life on the 22nd.

Marine Corps Returns to Original Ships: Last month, the bandit situation in Nengyi was tense. New Daming Sinking Ship, Trying to Salvage: On February 28 of the lunar calendar in the 17th year of the Republic of China, the New Daming merchant ship of the Lei Tong Company was sunk by the Japanese merchant ship Atsuta Maru in the Taixing port area. Negotiations in this case have been going on for a long time. Now Datong Company has hired more than ten divers and took a boat to the port to salvage the sunken ship the day before yesterday. On the 20th, when passing through Jiangyin, the Yidu Bureau asked the divers to go to Huangtiangang Port to try to salvage a coal ship. Due to time constraints, the divers went into the water to investigate, and then went to the port in the afternoon.

Homicide Case Expected to be Finalized: Hu Hongsheng, who opened a jade workshop in Daqiao Town, killed his apprentice Zhu Dajiu. His father Qilin sued the county, interrogated and detained the murderer and waited for legal action. It has been more than a year, but no sentence has been passed. Calligraphy and Painting Under the Peony Flowers of Tianning Temple: The abbot of Tianning Temple, Rangzhi, sent a letter to the calligraphers and painters of this city, Jin Jianwu and Gu Bokui, to visit the temple because the peonies were in full bloom. The Fourth Day of the Education Strike for Salary: The education in this county has been suspended this time, and another week has passed in an instant. To this day, there is still no hope of a complete resumption of classes. Yesterday (19th), the Education Association held an executive committee meeting and decided on three things on the spot: (1) Rectify the original income, such as land rent must be re-bid, miscellaneous donations must be strictly organized, and additional taxes must not be in arrears by the clerks. (2) Dismiss redundant personnel, all nominal and useless redundant personnel and redundant personnel not in the academic system should be dismissed together. (3) When the director takes office or hands over, there must be no remuneration and departure gunshots, and all kinds of strange phenomena that tarnish the purity of the education community. After the resolution, a letter was sent to the Education Bureau for reference.

Zhe Duo Town Plundered by Bandits: A few bandit boats suddenly came to Zhe Duo Town, which belongs to the county, at about 2:00 PM the day before yesterday. There were many bandits on board, all carrying guns. After landing, they searched every household in the town and set fire to several houses, shooting and wounding two farmers, Miao and Shen. The loss was estimated to be tens of thousands of yuan.

Ming Dynasty Porcelain Discovered in Desolate Tomb: The Construction Bureau of this county is now ordered to conscript workers to build roads. However, there are many desolate tombs in the Gaoluyingcheng area. Yesterday (18th) at 4:00 PM, a road construction worker suddenly dug up an ancient coffin with a pair of porcelain bowls and a porcelain jar inside, all of which were light yellow in color and had the words "Hongwu" on the bottom. Later, a gentleman bought it for ten yuan.

Tragic News in a Year of Famine: Xu, a woman from Shuangju Township in this county, hanged herself because it was difficult to make a living due to the high price of rice and firewood. By the time the neighbors rushed to rescue her, she had been dead for a long time.

Yancheng

Xingye Electric Light Company Scheduled to Close: The Yancheng Xingye Electric Light Company was prepared in the 9th year of the Republic of China, originally for the purpose of revitalizing local industries. Unfortunately, in the winter of the 15th year of the Republic of China, the machinery was burned by a neighboring fire, so the plan could not be realized. Now, the shareholders of the company, Xu Dichuan, Liao Gongyuan, etc., have requested the Yancheng County Government to appoint Xiao Biwen as the liquidator to be responsible for liquidation in order to end the company. All original managerial duties are legally terminated. From now on, all actions concerning the company will be handled by the liquidator, and it is scheduled to hold a shareholders' meeting at the Yancheng County Chamber of Commerce on June 16th to discuss the liquidation method.

The Bandit Situation is Still Very Rampant: Yancheng is rich in handmade products and has many schools (more than 500 in total). It was originally a happy land by the sea. Unexpectedly, in recent years, famines have occurred frequently. In addition, the Ma Camp was disbanded (the Ma Yuren Division of the former Huaiyang Protectorate Army), and the number of maritime people increased. As a result, petty thieves abounded and the country was full of bandits. Robbery and kidnapping occurred endlessly. Not only was it difficult for the rich to live in peace, but even middle-class families were uneasy. Recently, the Dada Liner, which runs from Yancheng to Shaobo, has been robbed a total of five times since the beginning of February this year. The Dasheng Liner, which runs from Yancheng to Taizhou, was also patronized by bandits once. All kinds of disturbances are too difficult to describe.

Jiashan

Monks Arrested and Religious Processions Prohibited: At Dongyue Temple and Qilaoye Temple in Xitang Town, religious processions are held on the 29th day of the lunar March every year. The town's party department, due to the unstable situation and frequent robberies, requested the county government to strictly prohibit them, and arrested the monks Bao Cheng and De Jing living in the temple and detained them in the county bureau. It also sent people to Xitang to persuade the stores to stop the religious procession. As for the detained monks, they will only be released after the religious procession is over.

County Government Convenes District Division Meeting: County Magistrate Shen Guangxiong convened a district division meeting in the county on the afternoon of the 19th. It was decided that the first district is the urban area of Yong'an Ganqiao, with district chief Li Bingzong, the second district is Fengjing Zhanghui Dayun Temple, with district chief Zhang Xingeng, the third district is Xitang Yuyao Dingzha, with district chief Lu Baozhi, and the fourth district is Taozhuang Tianren Hongjiawan Yangmiao, with district chief Fu Jinkui. It was unanimously approved.

Pinghu

Examination for County Magistrate Passes Physical Examination: For this third examination for county magistrates in this province, the local people who registered for the examination were Gao Chichang, the first section chief of the county government, Zhu Zhilai, and the secretary Li Guangye. According to Hangzhou News, a physical examination was held on the 18th. A total of 268 people passed the examination. It is said that Mr. Gao and Section Chief Zhu also passed the examination. Bandit Traces Found in Qingyanghui: At about 8:00 AM on the 18th, twenty-eight bandit boats came from the Xin Kaihe River to Qingyanghui in Xindai, carrying about 200 bandits, all of whom were armed and had several cannons, and went to Mingzhu'an. They had lunch at Yuqitang and then went from Hengmatou to Shantang. It seemed that they were going to Liujiayan Bridge. The Provincial Security Team stationed in Chenghuang Temple heard the news and transported them to Xincang on the Jiufeng Small Wheel to suppress the bandits.

Huzhou

Two Towns in Xixiang Robbed and Plundered by Bandits: Xiaoxikou in Changxing, which belongs to Huzhou, has many wealthy merchants and people, so it is coveted by bandits. At 12:00 PM on the night of the 18th, several bandit boats suddenly came, with fifty or sixty bandits, each holding wooden shell guns, swarming ashore and rushing into the market. Dozens of shots were fired. The firearms of the local security group had been robbed by bandits a few days ago, so there was no resistance. The bandits robbed and plundered at will. More than half of the seventy stores in the town were robbed. It seemed that thirty stores, such as Jingcheng Cloth Store, Hengyuan Dong Sauce Garden, and Wu Dachang, were robbed. The loss was about 20,000 to 30,000 yuan. At about 10:00 PM on the night of the 18th at Xucang Bridge, more than thirty bandits suddenly came, traveling on two Wushan boats and several Jiangbei civilian boats. After landing, several bandits guarded the east and west entrances of the town, and the remaining bandits searched the stores. Stores such as Aoxi Chengjing Goods Store, Jisheng Store, Yu Hengtai, and Chen Dingfeng, as well as more than ten residents such as Wu Manting, were not spared. The loss was nearly 10,000 yuan. However, Wu Manting, a gentry in Xucang Bridge, had a son who was a teacher in a primary school in Changxing. Manting hired a boat to Changxing to see his son on the morning of the 17th. When passing through Hengtang Ferry, six bandits suddenly stood on the shore with guns and threatened to stop the boat. The bandits got off the boat and tied up Wu Manting. There is still no news of him. Suddenly, the next day, his family was robbed by bandits, and all the more than fifty dan of rice and clothes were looted.

Hangzhou

Hiring Debt Raising Committee Members: The Zhejiang Provincial Government started raising construction bonds, and yesterday specially hired 40 members of the debt raising committee, mostly well-known figures in the economic circles of the province and other provinces, such as Jin Baishun, Zhang Renfu, Zhang Xuren, Wang Xiangquan, Wang Zhuqi, Mi Tingfang, and the presidents of the Jiaxing Wuxing Shaoxing Ningbo Chambers of Commerce, were all among those hired.

Regulations on the Proportion of Sugar Donations in the Province: The sugar donation in Zhejiang Province is implemented as a provincial office, and the director has been ordered to set up an office at the Sanqiao Zhizhixia to collect taxes. The proportion of donations was stipulated by the provincial government yesterday, with an annual amount of 544,800 yuan. The collection fee is set at 36,000 yuan, and the average monthly allocation is limited to 3,000 yuan.

Dahua Slider Allowed Exclusive Operation: The Zhejiang Construction Department, according to Dahua Slider Company's presentation, researched successfully and requested exclusive operation for ten years, and specially formulated five protection laws, and forwarded them to the provincial government for resolution, allowing exclusive operation for ten years.

Regulations on Short-Term Loans for the Qianye Industry: The Hangzhou Qianye industry held a meeting of colleagues in Liucui Jingxiang yesterday to discuss the matter of granting six pairs of long-term loans. It was decided that the loan granting date should be from April 28 to November 19 of the lunar calendar this year, which has a leap month, and one pair should be granted according to the regulations, for a total of seven pairs and nineteen days. The price of each large dish is ten yuan and five jiao per thousand yuan, totaling seventy-three yuan and five jiao per thousand yuan.

Xiaoshan

County Government's Request for Loan Repayment: Xiaoshan borrowed 10,000 yuan from various commercial firms in the city to handle land reports last fall due to lack of funds. It was to be paid in three installments, and also to be repaid in three installments. Later, the commercial firms were in urgent need of the last installment at the end of the year and were unable to raise the funds, so they borrowed the tenth and eleventh installments, totaling 6,375 yuan. The installment due at the end of January was used to offset the installment due at the end of December, and the remaining two installments should be repaid on time. Unexpectedly, the deadline has long passed, and the government has not heard from them. The commercial firms jointly submitted a petition to the County Chamber of Commerce and forwarded it to the County Government, requesting prompt repayment to alleviate the difficulties of the merchants.

Loan and Property Committee Recovers Fish Pond Donations: Many fish farmers in Xiaoshan have not yet paid the fish pond education rent and donations from last year. Now it is the season for rice planting in the spring of this year. Since last year's rent and donations have not been paid, this year's rent and donations must be continued. Yesterday, the Public Loan and Public Property Acceptance Committee specially sent a letter to the County Government requesting that the police be sent to the rural areas to strictly urge payment from household to household in order to close the case.

Three Deaths from Eating White Turtle: The family of Fu Jingchun, a fisherman from Chen Yuhu in the Hutou area of Xixiang, Xiaoshan, caught a white turtle weighing about one catty and fourteen taels in Baima Lake on the 18th. He cooked it and ate it at home. At midnight, his wife and daughter, a total of three people, were poisoned and died.

Page 11

The Seventh Day of the National Education Conference

The Fourth General Meeting was Held Yesterday

Temporary Proposal on Literacy Campaign Passed

Three Plans for Junior High School Social Education Discussed

The Fifth General Meeting will Continue this Morning

Closing Ceremony in the Afternoon after the General Meeting Tomorrow Morning

The Situation of the Fourth General Meeting Yesterday

Yesterday was the seventh day of the National Education Conference, and the fourth general meeting was held, as well as a meeting to review education expenses. The situation is recorded below.

Opening Situation

The bell rang at 2:00 PM to open the meeting. The chairman was still Vice President Chen Hexian. First, he respectfully read the General's Instructions. All stood in silence. Next, the case of Wu Zhihui and others' temporary proposal to request the Ministry of Education to actively promote the literacy campaign in the shortest possible time was opened for discussion.

Discussion on Literacy Campaign Proposal

▲Passed without Dissent

Liu Zhanen stood up and said that if there was no dissent, this case would be considered passed. The chairman asked, and the public had no dissent, so it was considered passed.

Discussion of Elementary Education Plan

｜Resolutions｜

(1) Kindergartens should all be run by Chinese people.

(2) Health education should involve special training.

(3) Moral education and curriculum must be separated.

(4) Elementary schools and kindergartens should, as a principle, be free of charge.

(5) Each province may establish special schools.

▲Establishment

Xiong Mengfei said that, after reviewing the report, the sixth item under the establishment section, that elementary education in any country should be run by nationals, and that foreigners absolutely cannot be allowed to run it arbitrarily, should be retained. Chen Dezheng, Li Zhaohuan, and others seconded the motion.

Wei Tingsheng said that this point must be considered. If the abolition of extraterritoriality does not allow foreigners to establish elementary schools, then the problem of education for the children of foreign nationals will cause panic. Therefore, there is no need to retain this item. We only need to develop our national compulsory education so that Chinese children do not enter foreign schools.

Liu Zhan'en said that currently, the large, medium, and small schools within China that were originally run by foreigners are now all presided over by Chinese people. As long as they do not violate the Chinese education regulations, they can be allowed to establish schools. At a time when promoting universal education, it is especially necessary to allow these schools to exist to help promote compulsory education.

Tao Xuan said that Mr. Wei's concern that if item six is deleted, foreigners who want to educate their own children will not be able to establish elementary schools is an overestimation. Elementary schools and kindergartens are basic education, and it is necessary to ensure that they are run by nationals.

Huang Jianzhong said that item six under the establishment section is the most important issue in this plan. This representative believes that it is necessary to retain it. The reasons have already been stated by Mr. Xiong and Mr. Tao. Moreover, foreign religious families instill their beliefs from a young age. Therefore, education in early childhood is a critical period for shaping character, and caution must be exercised. If this is not done, the spirit of the Three Principles of the People will be lost.

Xie Shuying said that Christian-run education has 6,890 institutions.

After a long discussion, the majority passed a motion to maintain the original plan (the original plan was "Non-Chinese people or organizations not entirely composed of Chinese people shall not establish elementary schools or kindergartens. Teachers and staff of elementary schools and kindergartens shall be limited to people who are entirely citizens of the Republic of China.")

▲Curriculum

Jin Baoshan said that it is difficult for doctors to be responsible for health education under item nine. There are only two or three such people in the world, so there should be special training to cultivate suitable talents. Jin then used a mimeographed paper to attach Wei Que's proposal to Jin Baoshan's proposal, believing that the education of the Three Principles of the People must pay attention to health education. Yu Ziyi seconded the motion and sent the written opinion to the drafting section of the assembly to revise the articles.

▲Moral Education

Chen Dezheng said that he opposes incorporating moral education into the curriculum. Under the Three Principles of the People, special attention must be paid to moral education. Therefore, it is appropriate to retain moral education as a separate item. Chen Heqin said that elementary education is different from middle school and university education. Therefore, it is appropriate to combine moral education and academic affairs into one to implement holistic education. Moral education and academic affairs cannot be separated.

Chen Dezheng said that the division of moral education and curriculum is not meant to be an absolute separation. The fear of establishing it separately is to show the importance of the spirit of the party.

Chen Heqin said that not only should moral education be based on the Three Principles of the People, but the curriculum should also be based on the Three Principles of the People. Therefore, combining them into one chapter of the curriculum does not harm the spirit of the party. Yu Ziyi said that the draft was separated, but the review committee merged them into one group. If the articles are merged according to the review committee, there will be inappropriate places. Therefore, he seconded Chen Dezheng's proposal and agreed to separate them. The chairman put it to a vote. The majority voted in favor of separating moral education.

▲Expenses

Chen Dezheng said that the review committee stipulated "no more than two yuan per semester." Can it be changed to "Elementary schools and kindergartens should, as a principle, be free of charge. In places with affluent local economies, fees may be charged at the discretion of the local authorities. Each city and county shall formulate regulations based on the local economic conditions of each elementary school and kindergarten, and submit them to the higher-level education administrative organs for approval and implementation." The majority passed the motion.

Zheng Hongnian proposed that the third item on expenses should be deleted. A minority did not pass the motion.

▲School Grade System

Chen Jianxiu said that the fourth item of the revised articles should be deleted because the establishment of special schools for children is mixed with social education. Therefore, it can be deleted. Meng Xiancheng seconded the motion. Wang Maozu said that education for the disabled is, according to international practice, included in social education. As for education for geniuses, it is included in ordinary elementary schools. The item is as follows: Each province should establish special schools, such as schools for geniuses, according to local needs and economic capabilities. Each city and county should establish special classes for children at their discretion.

Report from the Secondary Education Group

After the discussion on elementary education was completed, Chairman Liao Shicheng, on behalf of the Secondary Education Group, reported.

Section 3, Regulations for the Establishment of Secondary Schools,

Second Measure,

A. Change "shall not add" to "temporarily postpone adding", and add "except for provinces with annual education expenditures of more than 2 million yuan or only have one senior high school".

B. Delete "already has a plan (see Chapter 3)", add "etc." after domestic science, and change "can be included in the general department" to "can be jointly run with the general department depending on the circumstances".

C. Change to "Ratio of the number of general high schools and agricultural and industrial high schools in a province".

(1) The senior high school general department and the agricultural and industrial departments should each account for half of the total number of schools in principle.

(2) If the number of general high schools and agricultural and industrial high schools exceeds a ratio of three to one, at least the general high schools exceeding the ratio should be converted into agricultural or industrial departments during the political tutelage period.

J. Change "should be established in provinces that have not yet established" to "establish two high schools in each province, for a total of twenty schools. Except for eleven general departments, with one school in each province, the remaining schools will be seven agricultural departments and three industrial departments (the years and number of schools established for each department are detailed in the first and second budget tables listed below). The education departments of each province shall formulate school establishment plans based on the circumstances and submit them to the Ministry of Education for approval and implementation."

The education departments of each province shall formulate school establishment plans and submit them to the Ministry of Education for approval and implementation (not listed in the budget).
